Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Proceed directly to execution based on the classified tier.\n\n**Reference** — the tier keyword tables (for context only, do not re-classify):\n- **STRICT**: security, authentication, database, migration, refactor, breaking change, encrypt, token, session, oauth\n- **EXEMPT**: explain, search, commit, push, plan, discuss, brainstorm\n- **LIGHT**: typo, comment, whitespace, lint, docstring, formatting, minor\n- **STANDARD**: implement, add, create, update, fix, build, modify, change (default)\n\n### 2. Confidence Display (Human-Readable)\n\nAfter the mandatory classification header, show a human-readable summary:\n\n```\n**Tier: STANDARD** [████████░░] 80%\n\nClassified as STANDARD:\n- Keywords matched: add, implement\n- Confidence score: 0.78\n- Considered alternatives: STRICT (0.35)\n```\n\nIf confidence <70%, add prompt: \"⚠️ Low confidence. Override with: `--compliance [strict|standard|light|exempt]`\"\n\n**Note**: The machine-readable header (Section 0) is for telemetry/A/B testing. This human-readable display is for user understanding.\n\n### 3. Execution Phase\n\nExecute task according to tier requirements:\n\n**STRICT Execution**:\n1. Activate project (mcp__serena__activate_project)\n2. Verify git working directory clean (git status)\n3. Load codebase context (codebase-retrieval)\n4. Check relevant memories (list_memories -> read_memory)\n5. Identify all affected files and test files\n6. Make changes with full checklist\n7. Identify all files that import changed code\n8. Update all affected files\n9. Spawn verification agent (quality-engineer)\n10. Run comprehensive tests: `pytest [path] -v`\n11. Answer adversarial questions\n\n**STANDARD Execution**:\n1. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist keyword, documentation path)\n-> Quick sanity check only\n-> No verification delay\n```\n\n### EXEMPT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"explain how the auth flow works\"\n\n-> Classified as EXEMPT (explain classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide \"\"\"Tests for per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 3) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T02.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Task {i}\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T02.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _pass_factory(task, config, phase):\n        \"\"\"Subprocess factory that always succeeds with 3 turns consumed.\"\"\"\n        return (0, 3, 1024)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _fail_factory(task, config, phase):\n        \"\"\"Subprocess factory that always fails.\"\"\"\n        return (1, 5, 512)\n\n    def test_per_task_spawns_one_subprocess_per_task(self, tmp_path):\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(3)\n\n        spawn_count = [0]\n\n        def counting_factory(task, config, phase):\n            spawn_count[0] += 1\n            return (0, 2, 100)\n\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, _subprocess_factory=counting_factory\n        )\n        assert spawn_count[0] == 3\n        assert len(results) == 3\n        assert remaining == []\n\n    def test_per_task_all_pass(self, tmp_path):\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(2)\n\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, _subprocess_factory=self._pass_factory\n        )\n        assert all(r.status == TaskStatus.PASS for r in results)\n        assert remaining == []\n\n    def test_per_task_budget_prevents_starvation(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"If budget insufficient for next task, HALT with remaining task IDs.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(3)\n\n        # Budget allows only 1 task launch (min_allocation=5, budget=8)\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=8, minimum_allocation=5)\n\n        def consume_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 5, 100)\n\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=consume_factory,\n        )\n        # First task succeeds, next two should be skipped due to budget\n        passed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS]\n        skipped = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED]\n        assert len(passed) == 1\n        assert len(skipped) == 2\n        assert FAIL, 2 turns","+            (0, 5, 1536),    # PASS, 5 turns","+            (124, 4, 256),   # INCOMPLETE (timeout), 4 turns","+        ]","+        call_index = [0]","+","+        def mixed_factory(task, config, phase):","+            idx = call_index[0]","+            call_index[0] += 1","+            return outcomes[idx]","+","+        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)","+        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(","+            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,","+            _subprocess_factory=mixed_factory,","+        )","+","+        # Track per-task consumption: task 1=3, task 2=7, task 3=2, task 4=5, task 5=4\n        outcomes = [\n            (0, 3, 1024),    # PASS, 3 turns\n            (0, 7, 2048),    # PASS, 7 turns\n            (1, 2, 512),     # FAIL, 2 turns\n            (0, 5, 1536),    # PASS, 5 turns\n            (124, 4, 256),   # INCOMPLETE (timeout), 4 turns\n        ]\n        call_index = [0]\n\n        def mixed_factory(task, config, phase):\n            idx = call_index[0]\n            call_index[0] += 1\n            return outcomes[idx]\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=mixed_factory,\n        )\n\n        # All 5 tasks launched (no budget exhaustion)\n        assert len(results) == 5\n        assert remaining == []\n        assert call_index[0] == 5\n\n        # Verify per-task statuses\n        assert results[0].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[1].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[2].status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n        assert results[3].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[4].status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n\n        # Budget accounting: sum of per-task actual turns == total consumed\n        expected_total_consumed = 3 + 7 + 2 + 5 + 4  # = 21\n        assert ledger.consumed == expected_total_consumed\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - expected_total_consumed + ledger.reimbursed\n\n        # Aggregate into phase report\n        report = aggregate_task_results(\n            phase_number=1, task_results=results, remaining_task_ids=remaining\n        )\n        assert report.tasks_total == 5\n        assert report.tasks_passed == 3\n        assert report.tasks_failed == 1\n        assert report.tasks_incomplete == 1\n        assert report.status == \"PARTIAL\"\n        assert report.total_turns_consumed == sum(r.turns_consumed for r in results)\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_budget_exhaustion_skips_remaining(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Budget exhaustion after 3 tasks skips remaining 2.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # \"\"\"Tests for per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 3) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T02.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Task {i}\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T02.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _pass_factory(task, config, phase):\n        \"\"\"Subprocess factory that always succeeds with 3 turns consumed.\"\"\"\n        return (0, 3, 1024)\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _fail_factory(task, config, phase):\n        \"\"\"Subprocess factory that always fails.\"\"\"\n        return (1, 5, 512)\n\n    def test_per_task_spawns_one_subprocess_per_task(self, tmp_path):\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(3)\n\n        spawn_count = [0]\n\n        def counting_factory(task, config, phase):\n            spawn_count[0] += 1\n            return (0, 2, 100)\n\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, _subprocess_factory=counting_factory\n        )\n        assert spawn_count[0] == 3\n        assert len(results) == 3\n        assert remaining == []\n\n    def  tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=consume_factory,\n        )\n        # First task succeeds, next two should be skipped due to budget\n        passed = [r for r allocate → launch → collect → aggregate\n    with budget verification. (D-0012)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 5) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T03.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Integration Task {i}\",\n                description=f\"Test task {i} for integration\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T03.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_five_tasks_mixed_outcomes(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Full loop: 5 tasks with varied outcomes and budget accounting.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Track per-task consumption: task 1=3, task 2=7, task 3=2, task 4=5, task 5=4\n        outcomes = [\n            (0, 3, 1024),    # PASS, 3 turns\n            (0, 7, 2048),    # PASS, 7 turns\n            (1, 2, 512),     # FAIL, 2 turns\n            (0, 5, 1536),    # PASS, 5 turns\n            (124, 4, 256),   # INCOMPLETE (timeout), 4 turns\n        ]\n        call_index = [0]\n\n        def mixed_factory(task, config, phase):\n            idx = call_index[0]\n            call_index[0] += 1\n            return outcomes[idx]\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=mixed_factory,\n        )\n\n        # All 5 tasks launched (no budget exhaustion)\n        assert len(results) == 5\n        assert remaining == []\n        assert call_index[0] == 5\n\n        # Verify per-task statuses\n        assert results[0].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[1].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[2].status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n        assert results[3].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[4].status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n\n        # Budget accounting: available reflects actual turn consumption\n        # The executor pre-debits minimum_allocation (5) per task, then reconciles.\n        # For actual < pre-alloc: credit(pre-alloc - actual)\n        # For actual > pre-alloc: debit(actual - pre-alloc)\n        # Net effect on available: initial - sum(actual_turns) for all tasks\n        actual_turns = [3, 7, 2, 5, 4]\n        net_consumed = sum(actual_turns)  # 21\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - net_consumed + ledger.reimbursed - ledger.consumed + ledger.consumed\n        # Simpler: available = initial - consumed + reimbursed\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - ledger.consumed + ledger.reimbursed\n        # And the net effect is: available == initial - sum(actual)\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - net_consumed\n\n        # Aggregate into phase report\n        report = aggregate_task_results(\n            phase_number=1, task_results=results, remaining_task_ids=remaining\n        )\n        assert report.tasks_total == 5\n        assert report.tasks_passed == 3\n        assert report.tasks_failed == 1\n        assert report.tasks_incomplete == 1\n        assert report.status == \"PARTIAL\"\n        assert report.total_turns_consumed == sum(r.turns_consumed for r in results)\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_budget_exhaustion_skips_remaining(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Budget exhaustion after 3 tasks skips remaining 2.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Each task consumes 8 turns; budget=25, minimum_allocation=5\n        # Task 1: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=8, avail=17\n        # Task 2: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=16, avail=9\n        # Task 3: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=24, avail=1\n        # Task 4: can_launch? avail=1 < min_alloc=5 → SKIP\n        def heavy_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 8, 500)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=25, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=heavy_factory,\n        )\n\n        passed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS]\n        skipped = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED]\n        assert len(passed) == 3\n        assert len(skipped) == 2\n        assert remaining == [\"T03.04\", \"T03.05\"]\n\n        # allocate → launch → collect → aggregate\n    with budget verification. (D-0012)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 5) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T03.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Integration Task {i}\",\n                description=f\"Test task {i} for integration\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T03.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_five_tasks_mixed_outcomes(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Full loop: 5 tasks with varied outcomes and budget accounting.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Track per-task consumption: task 1=3, task 2=7, task 3=2, task 4=5, task 5=4\n        outcomes = [\n            (0, 3, 1024),    # PASS, 3 turns\n            (0, 7, 2048),    # PASS, 7 turns\n            (1, 2, 512),     # FAIL, 2 turns\n            (0, 5, 1536),    # PASS, 5 turns\n            (124, 4, 256),   # INCOMPLETE (timeout), 4 turns\n        ]\n        call_index = [0]\n\n        def mixed_factory(task, config, phase):\n            idx = call_index[0]\n            call_index[0] += 1\n            return outcomes[idx]\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=mixed_factory,\n        )\n\n        # All 5 tasks launched (no budget exhaustion)\n        assert len(results) == 5\n        assert remaining == []\n        assert call_index[0] == 5\n\n        # Verify per-task statuses\n        assert results[0].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[1].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[2].status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n        assert results[3].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[4].status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n\n        # Budget accounting: available reflects actual turn consumption\n        # The executor pre-debits minimum_allocation (5) per task, then reconciles.\n        # For actual < pre-alloc: credit(pre-alloc - actual)\n        # For actual > pre-alloc: debit(actual - pre-alloc)\n        # Net effect on available: initial - sum(actual_turns) for all tasks\n        actual_turns = [3, 7, 2, 5, 4]\n        net_consumed = sum(actual_turns)  # 21\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - net_consumed + ledger.reimbursed - ledger.consumed + ledger.consumed\n        # Simpler: available = initial - consumed + reimbursed\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - ledger.consumed + ledger.reimbursed\n        # And the net effect is: available == initial - sum(actual)\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - net_consumed\n\n        # Aggregate into phase report\n        report = aggregate_task_results(\n            phase_number=1, task_results=results, remaining_task_ids=remaining\n        )\n        assert report.tasks_total == 5\n        assert report.tasks_passed == 3\n        assert report.tasks_failed == 1\n        assert report.tasks_incomplete == 1\n        assert report.status == \"PARTIAL\"\n        assert report.total_turns_consumed == sum(r.turns_consumed for r in results)\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_budget_exhaustion_skips_remaining(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Budget exhaustion after 3 tasks skips remaining 2.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Each task consumes 8 turns; budget=25, minimum_allocation=5\n        # Task 1: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=8, avail=17\n        # Task 2: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=16, avail=9\n        # Task 3: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=24, avail=1\n        # Task 4: can_launch? avail=1 < min_alloc=5 → SKIP\n        def heavy_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 8, 500)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=25, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=heavy_factory,\n        )\n\n        passed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS]\n        skipped = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED]\n        assert len(passed) == 3\n        assert len(skipped) == 2\n        assert remaining == [\"T03.04\", \"T03.05\"]\n\n        # Aggregate reflects skipped tasks\n        report = aggregate_task_results(1, results, remaining)\n        assert report.tasks_total == 7  # 5 results + 2 remaining\n        assert report.tasks_skipped == 2\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_all_pass_aggregation(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"All 5 tasks pass → PASS status and CONTINUE recommendation.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        def pass_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 3, 1024)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=pass_factory,\n        )\n\n        assert all(r.status == TaskStatus.PASS for r in results)\n        assert remaining == []\n\n        report = aggregate_task_results(1, results, remaining)\n        assert report.status == \"PASS\"\n        md = report.to_markdown()\n        assert \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in md\n        assert \"tasks_total: 5\" in md\n        assert \"tasks_passed: 5\" in md\n\n        # Budget: 5 tasks * 3 turns each = 15 net consumed\n        # available = initial - net consumed = 100 - 15 = 85\n        assert ledger.available() == 85\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":989,"oldLines":16,"newStart":989,"newLines":12,"lines":[" ","         # Launch claude -p subprocess\\\\n    2. Start output monitor thread\\\\n    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\\\\n    4. Parse result file for CONTINUE/HALT\\\\n    5. Record PhaseResult\\\\n    6. Decide whether to continue or halt\\\\n    \\\\\\\"\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\"\\\\n    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\\\\n    if shutil.which(\\\\\\\"claude\\\\\\\") is None:\\\\n        raise SystemExit(\\\\n            \\\\\\\"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \\\\\\\"\\\\n            \\\\\\\"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\\\\\\\"\\\\n        )\\\\n\\\\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\\\\n    signal_handler.install()\\\\n\\\\n    setup_debug_logger(config)\\\\n    import logging as _logging\\\\n    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\\\\n\\\\n    logger = SprintLogger(config)\\\\n    tui = SprintTUI(config)\\\\n    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\\\\\\\"/dev/null\\\\\\\"))  # reset per phase\\\\n    proc_manager: ClaudeProcess | None = None\\\\n\\\\n    sprint_result = SprintResult(config=config)\\\\n    logger.write_header(sprint_result)\\\\n\\\\n    tui.start()\\\\n\\\\n    try:\\\\n        for phase in config.active_phases:\\\\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\\\\n                sprint_result.outcome = SprintOutcome.INTERRUPTED\\\\n                break\\\\n\\\\n            # Reset monitor for this phase\\\\n            output_path = config.output_file(phase)\\\\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\\\\n            monitor.start()\\\\n\\\\n            # Update tmux tail pane if running in tmux\\\\n            if config.tmux_session_name:\\\\n                update_tail_pane(config.tmux_session_name, output_path)\\\\n\\\\n            # Launch claude\\\\n            proc_manager = ClaudeProcess(config, phase)\\\\n            proc_manager.start()\\\\n            started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\\\\n            # Use monotonic clock for deadline enforcement to be immune to NTP adjustments\\\\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + proc_manager.timeout_seconds\\\\n            logger.write_phase_start(phase, started_at)\\\\n\\\\n            debug_log(_dbg, \\\\\\\"PHASE_BEGIN\\\\\\\", phase=phase.number, file=str(phase.file))\\\\n\\\\n            tui.update(sprint_result, monitor.state, phase)\\\\n\\\\n            # Poll loop: wait for process to finish while updating TUI\\\\n            # Enforces monotonic timeout via deadline check.\\\\n            _timed_out = False\\\\n            _stall_acted = False  # single-fire guard for watchdog\\\\n            _poll_start = time.monotonic()\\\\n            while proc_manager._process.poll() is None:\\\\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\\\\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\\\\n                    break\\\\n                if time.monotonic() > deadline:\\\\n                    # Timeout reached: kill the process, exit loop\\\\n                    _timed_out = True\\\\n                    proc_manager.terminate()\\\\n                    break\\\\n\\\\n                ms = monitor.state\\\\n                _elapsed = time.monotonic() - _poll_start\\\\n\\\\n                debug_log(\\\\n                    _dbg,\\\\n                    \\\\\\\"poll_tick\\\\\\\",\\\\n                    phase=phase.number,\\\\n                    pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\\\\n                    poll_result=\\\\\\\"running\\\\\\\",\\\\n                    elapsed=round(_elapsed, 1),\\\\n                    output_bytes=ms.output_bytes,\\\\n                    growth_rate=round(ms.growth_rate_bps, 1),\\\\n                    stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\\\\n                    stall_status=ms.stall_status,\\\\n                )\\\\n\\\\n                # --- Watchdog: stall timeout check ---\\\\n                if (\\\\n                    config.stall_timeout > 0\\\\n                    and ms.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\\\\n                    and ms.events_received > 0  # don't trigger during startup\\\\n                    and not _stall_acted\\\\n                ):\\\\n                    _stall_acted = True\\\\n                    debug_log(\\\\n                        _dbg,\\\\n                        \\\\\\\"watchdog_triggered\\\\\\\",\\\\n                        phase=phase.number,\\\\n                        action=config.stall_action,\\\\n                        stall_seconds=round(ms.stall_seconds, 1),\\\\n                        pid=proc_manager._process.pid,\\\\n                    )\\\\n                    if config.stall_action == \\\\\\\"kill\\\\\\\":\\\\n                        import sys\\\\n                        print(\\\\n                            f\\\\\\\"[WATCHDOG] Stall detected ({ms.stall_seconds:.0f}s > \\\\\\\"\\\\n                            f\\\\\\\"{config.stall_timeout}s) — killing phase {phase.number}\\\\\\\",\\\\n                            file=sys.stderr,\\\\n                        )\\\\n                        _timed_out = True\\\\n                        proc_manager.terminate()\\\\n                        break\\\\n                    else:\\\\n                        # per task\n\n        results, _ = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=factory,\n        )\n        # 2 tasks * 7 turns = 14 back.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = [TaskEntry(task_id=\"T02.01\", title=\"Task 1\")]\n        ledger = (D-0012)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 5) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T03.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Integration Task {i}\",\n                description=f\"Test task {i} for integration\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T03.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_five_tasks_mixed_outcomes(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Full loop: 5 tasks with varied outcomes and budget accounting.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Track per-task consumption: task 1=3, task 2=7, task 3=2, task 4=5, task 5=4\n        outcomes = [\n            (0, 3, 1024),    # PASS, 3 turns\n            (0, 7, 2048),    # PASS, 7 turns\n            (1, 2, 512),     # FAIL, 2 turns\n            (0, 5, 1536),    # PASS, 5 turns\n            (124, 4, 256),   # INCOMPLETE (timeout), 4 turns\n        ]\n        call_index = [0]\n\n        def mixed_factory(task, config, phase):\n            idx = call_index[0]\n            call_index[0] += 1\n            return outcomes[idx]\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=mixed_factory,\n        )\n\n        # All 5 tasks launched (no budget exhaustion)\n        assert len(results) == 5\n        assert remaining == []\n        assert call_index[0] == 5\n\n        # Verify per-task statuses\n        assert results[0].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[1].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[2].status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n        assert results[3].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[4].status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n\n        # Budget accounting: available reflects actual turn consumption\n        # The executor pre-debits minimum_allocation (5) per task, then reconciles.\n        # Net effect on available: initial - sum(actual_turns)\n        actual_turns = [3, 7, 2, 5, 4]\n        net_consumed = sum(actual_turns)  # 21\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - net_consumed  # = 79\n        # Verify internal accounting is consistent\n        assert ledger.available() == ledger.initial_budget - ledger.consumed + ledger.reimbursed\n\n        # Aggregate into phase report\n        report = aggregate_task_results(\n            phase_number=1, task_results=results, remaining_task_ids=remaining\n        )\n        assert report.tasks_total == 5\n        assert report.tasks_passed == 3\n        assert report.tasks_failed == 1\n        assert report.tasks_incomplete == 1\n        assert report.status == \"PARTIAL\"\n        assert report.total_turns_consumed == sum(r.turns_consumed for r in results)\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_budget_exhaustion_skips_remaining(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Budget exhaustion after 3 tasks skips remaining 2.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Each task consumes 8 turns; budget=25, minimum_allocation=5\n        # Task 1: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=8, avail=17\n        # Task 2: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=16, avail=9\n        # Task 3: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=24, avail=1\n        # Task 4: can_launch? avail=1 < min_alloc=5 → SKIP\n        def heavy_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 8, 500)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=25, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=heavy_factory,\n        )\n\n        passed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS]\n        skipped = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED]\n        assert len(passed) == 3\n        assert len(skipped) == 2\n        assert remaining == [\"T03.04\", \"T03.05\"]\n\n        # allocate → launch → collect → aggregate\n    with budget verification. (D-0012)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _make_tasks(count: int = 5) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n        return [\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=f\"T03.{i:02d}\",\n                title=f\"Integration Task {i}\",\n                description=f\"Test task {i} for integration\",\n                dependencies=[f\"T03.{i-1:02d}\"] if i > 1 else [],\n            )\n            for i in range(1, count + 1)\n        ]\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_five_tasks_mixed_outcomes(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Full loop: 5 tasks with varied outcomes and budget accounting.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Track per-task consumption: task 1=3, task 2=7, task 3=2, task 4=5, task 5=4\n        outcomes = [\n            (0, 3, 1024),    # PASS, 3 turns\n            (0, 7, 2048),    # PASS, 7 turns\n            (1, 2, 512),     # FAIL, 2 turns\n            (0, 5, 1536),    # PASS, 5 turns\n            (124, 4, 256),   # INCOMPLETE (timeout), 4 turns\n        ]\n        call_index = [0]\n\n        def mixed_factory(task, config, phase):\n            idx = call_index[0]\n            call_index[0] += 1\n            return outcomes[idx]\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=mixed_factory,\n        )\n\n        # All 5 tasks launched (no budget exhaustion)\n        assert len(results) == 5\n        assert remaining == []\n        assert call_index[0] == 5\n\n        # Verify per-task statuses\n        assert results[0].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[1].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[2].status == TaskStatus.FAIL\n        assert results[3].status == TaskStatus.PASS\n        assert results[4].status == TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n\n        # Budget accounting: available reflects actual turn consumption\n        # The executor pre-debits minimum_allocation (5) per task, then reconciles.\n        # Net effect on available: initial - sum(actual_turns)\n        actual_turns = [3, 7, 2, 5, 4]\n        net_consumed = sum(actual_turns)  # 21\n        assert ledger.available() == 100 - net_consumed  # = 79\n        # Verify internal accounting is consistent\n        assert ledger.available() == ledger.initial_budget - ledger.consumed + ledger.reimbursed\n\n        # Aggregate into phase report\n        report = aggregate_task_results(\n            phase_number=1, task_results=results, remaining_task_ids=remaining\n        )\n        assert report.tasks_total == 5\n        assert report.tasks_passed == 3\n        assert report.tasks_failed == 1\n        assert report.tasks_incomplete == 1\n        assert report.status == \"PARTIAL\"\n        assert report.total_turns_consumed == sum(r.turns_consumed for r in results)\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_budget_exhaustion_skips_remaining(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Budget exhaustion after 3 tasks skips remaining 2.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        # Each task consumes 8 turns; budget=25, minimum_allocation=5\n        # Task 1: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=8, avail=17\n        # Task 2: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=16, avail=9\n        # Task 3: debit 5 upfront, then adjust to 8 → consumed=24, avail=1\n        # Task 4: can_launch? avail=1 < min_alloc=5 → SKIP\n        def heavy_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 8, 500)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=25, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=heavy_factory,\n        )\n\n        passed = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.PASS]\n        skipped = [r for r in results if r.status == TaskStatus.SKIPPED]\n        assert len(passed) == 3\n        assert len(skipped) == 2\n        assert remaining == [\"T03.04\", \"T03.05\"]\n\n        # Aggregate reflects skipped tasks\n        report = aggregate_task_results(1, results, remaining)\n        assert report.tasks_total == 7  # 5 results + 2 remaining\n        assert report.tasks_skipped == 2\n\n    def test_integration_subprocess_all_pass_aggregation(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"All 5 tasks pass → PASS status and CONTINUE recommendation.\"\"\"\n        config = _make_config(tmp_path, num_phases=1)\n        phase = config.phases[0]\n        tasks = self._make_tasks(5)\n\n        def pass_factory(task, config, phase):\n            return (0, 3, 1024)\n\n        ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=100, minimum_allocation=5)\n        results, remaining = execute_phase_tasks(\n            tasks, config, phase, ledger=ledger,\n            _subprocess_factory=pass_factory,\n        )\n\n        assert all(r.status == TaskStatus.PASS for r in results)\n        assert remaining == []\n\n        report = aggregate_task_results(1, results, remaining)\n        assert report.status == \"PASS\"\n        md = report.to_markdown()\n        assert \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in md\n        assert \"tasks_total: 5\" in md\n        assert \"tasks_passed: 5\" in md\n\n        #
